001|# Product Requirement Document for Object Tracking Sports App
002|
003|## Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: Python
006|- **Project Name**: object_tracking_sports_app
007|
008|## Original Requirements
009|Create a Python program to optimize object tracking and real-time video overlays for a sports app utilizing YOLO, ONNX, and a hybrid LLM, ensuring compatibility for mobile device use.
010|
011|
012|## Product Definition
013|
014|### Product Goals
015|- Goal 1: Optimize object tracking for enhanced accuracy
016|- Goal 2: Implement real-time video overlays for engaging user experience
017|- Goal 3: Ensure seamless compatibility for mobile devices
018|
019|### User Stories
020|1. As a sports fan, I want to see real-time player tracking during a game to enhance my viewing experience.
021|2. As a coach, I want to analyze player movements through video overlays for better training sessions.
022|3. As a sports app user, I want smooth performance on my mobile device while using the tracking features.
023|
024|### Competitive Analysis
025|- Product A: Pros - Advanced object tracking technology, Cons - Limited mobile compatibility
026|- Product B: Pros - Real-time video overlays, Cons - Lack of YOLO integration
027|- Product C: Pros - Hybrid LLM implementation, Cons - Slow performance on mobile devices
028|
029|### Technical Specifications
030|
031|#### Requirements Analysis
032|- Utilize YOLO for object detection to enhance tracking accuracy.
033|- Implement ONNX for model optimization to ensure performance on mobile devices.
034|- Integrate a hybrid LLM for real-time data processing and analysis.
035|
036|#### Requirements Pool
037|- P0: Must have YOLO and ONNX integration.
038|- P1: Should have real-time video overlay functionality.
039|- P2: Nice to have additional analytics features for user engagement.
040|
041|#### UI Design Draft
042|- Basic layout includes a video feed area, overlay display for tracked objects, and user controls for settings.
043|
044|#### Open Questions
045|- What specific mobile devices should we target for compatibility?
046|- Are there any specific performance metrics we need to meet?
047|
